(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types
    agent
    receptacle
    object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (not (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (at ?a ?r)
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?a ?r)
    :effect (open ?r)
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (holding ?a ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (not (holding ?a ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect ()
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (clean ?o)
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (sliced ?o)
  )
)

(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (not (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (at ?a ?r)
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?a ?r)
    :effect (open ?r)
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (holding ?a ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (not (holding ?a ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (and)
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (clean ?o)
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (sliced ?o)
  )
)

This is the previous domain file (df):
(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (not (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (at ?a ?r)
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?a ?r)
    :effect (open ?r)
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (holding ?a ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (not (holding ?a ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (and)
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (clean ?o)
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (sliced ?o)
  )
)

This is the previous problem file (pf):

(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (not (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (at ?a ?r)
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?a ?r)
    :effect (open ?r)
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (holding ?a ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (not (holding ?a ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (and)
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)

This is the previous domain file (df):
(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (not (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (at ?a ?r)
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?a ?r)
    :effect (open ?r)
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (holding ?a ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (not (holding ?a ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (and)
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (clean ?o)
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (sliced ?o)
  )
)

(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (not (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (at ?a ?r)
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?a ?r)
    :effect (open ?r)
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (holding ?a ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (not (holding ?a ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (and)
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)

    :effect (clean ?o)
  )

(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (not (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (at ?a ?r)
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?a ?r)
    :effect (open ?r)
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (holding ?a ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (not (holding ?a ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (and)
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (clean ?o)
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )

    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)

This is the previous domain file (df):
(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (not (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (at ?a ?r)
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?a ?r)
    :effect (open ?r)
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (holding ?a ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (not (holding ?a ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (and)
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (clean ?o)
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (sliced ?o)
  )
)

This is the previous domain file (df):
(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (not (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (at ?a ?r)
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?a ?r)
    :effect (open ?r)
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (holding ?a ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (not (holding ?a ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (and)
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (clean ?o)
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (sliced ?o)
  )
)

This is the previous domain file (df):
(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (not (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (at ?a ?r)
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?a ?r)
    :effect (open ?r)
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (holding ?a ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (not (holding ?a ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (and)
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (clean ?o)
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (sliced ?o)
  )
)

This is the previous domain file (df):
(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (not (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (at ?a ?r)
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?a ?r)
    :effect (open ?r)
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (holding ?a ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (not (holding ?a ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (and)
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (clean ?o)
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (sliced ?o)
  )
)

(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (not (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (at ?a ?r)
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?a ?r)
    :effect (open ?r)
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (holding ?a ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (not (holding ?a ?o)))
  )

  )

This is the previous domain file (df):
(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (not (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (at ?a ?r)
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?a ?r)
    :effect (open ?r)
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (holding ?a ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (not (holding ?a ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (and)
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (clean ?o)
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (sliced ?o)
  )
)

(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (not (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (at ?a ?r)
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (not (open ?r)))
    :effect (open ?r)
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)

This is the previous domain file (df):
(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (not (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (at ?a ?r)
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (not (open ?r)))
    :effect (open ?r)
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (holding ?a ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (not (holding ?a ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (and)
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (clean ?o)
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (sliced ?o)
  )
)

This is the previous domain file (df):
(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (not (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (at ?a ?r)
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (not (open ?r)))
    :effect (open ?r)
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (holding ?a ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (not (holding ?a ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (and)
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (clean ?o)
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (sliced ?o)
  )
)

(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (not (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (at ?a ?r)
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (not (open ?r)))
    :effect (open ?r)
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (holding ?a ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (not (holding ?a ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (and)
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )

    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)

This is the previous domain file (df):
(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (not (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (at ?a ?r)
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (not (open ?r)))
    :effect (open ?r)
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (holding ?a ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (not (holding ?a ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (and)
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (clean ?o)
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (sliced ?o)
  )
)

(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (not (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (at ?a ?r)
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (not (open ?r)))
    :effect (open ?r)
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (holding ?a ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (not (holding ?a ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (and)
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (clean ?o)
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (sliced ?o)
  )
)

This is the previous domain file (df):
(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (not (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (at ?a ?r)
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (not (open ?r)))
    :effect (open ?r)
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (holding ?a ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (not (holding ?a ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (and)
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (clean ?o)
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (sliced ?o)
  )
)

This is the previous domain file (df):
(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (not (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (at ?a ?r)
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (not (open ?r)))
    :effect (open ?r)
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (holding ?a ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (not (holding ?a ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (and)
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (clean ?o)
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (sliced ?o)
  )
)

(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (not (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (at ?a ?r)
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (not (open ?r)))
    :effect (open ?r)
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (holding ?a ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (not (holding ?a ?o)))

    :precondition (not (at ?a ?r))

  )

    :effect (open ?r)
  )

This is the previous domain file (df):
(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (not (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (at ?a ?r)
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (not (open ?r)))
    :effect (open ?r)
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (holding ?a ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (not (holding ?a ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (and)
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (clean ?o)
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (sliced ?o)
  )
)

(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (not (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (at ?a ?r)
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (not (open ?r)))
    :effect (open ?r)
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (holding ?a ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)

This is the previous domain file (df):
(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (not (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (at ?a ?r)
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (not (open ?r)))
    :effect (open ?r)
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (holding ?a ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (not (holding ?a ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (and)
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (clean ?o)
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (sliced ?o)
  )
)

This is the previous domain file (df):
(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (not (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (at ?a ?r)
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (not (open ?r)))
    :effect (open ?r)
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (holding ?a ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (not (holding ?a ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (and)
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (clean ?o)
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?a ?o)
    :effect (sliced ?o)
  )
)
